Home Truein Help and Support Leaves How to give leave eligibility after probation period? How to give leave eligibility after probation period? You can give leave eligibility by enabling policy lo allocate leaves after X days of joining for the particular leave type. Home Truein Help and Support Leaves How to allot comp off leaves? How to allot comp off leaves? To allott and configure comp off leaves you can do this via two ways – One by one from -> Leaves -> Manage Leaves -> Allot Leave -> Select Leave type as CompOff – Via Spreadsheet you can download the sheet -> In leave type write CompOff -> Allott numbers -> Reupload the sheet back Products Open menu Industry Open menu Solutions Open menu Pricing Customer Stories About Us Company Open menu Login Schedule a Demo Why Truein Face Attendance Testimonials Proudly powered by WordPress . Home Truein Help and Support Leaves Need to allot Sick leaves at once for the year, casual leaves on half yearly basis. How can I do it? Need to allot Sick leaves at once for the year, casual leaves on half yearly basis. How can I do it? Admin can define the leave policies from Web dashboard > Leaves > Setup Leaves > Leave policies. While defining the Sick Leave and Casual Leave you can select the “Allot Leaves on Yearly, Half yearly basis” respectively. Home Truein Help and Support Leaves Can we setup flexi holidays? Can we setup flexi holidays? Yes, admins can set up flexi holiday Login to Dashboard > Leaves > Holiday > Holiday Policy > Set flexi leaves. Alternatively you can do the same in workforce planning as well. Home Truein Help and Support Leaves How to setup Time off (Leave) Module on new site? How to setup Time off (Leave) Module on new site? Every organization has its leave types and leave policies. You can set up your entire time off (leave) management in the Truein time off(leave) module. If your organization has different leave policies for different categories of staff, then follow steps 1.1 and 1.2; else, skip these steps. E.g. Permanent staff is eligible for 12 casual leaves a year; Intern staff is eligible for 6 casual leaves, and Temporary staff is not eligible for any casual leave. Step 1.1: Setup Categories (Optional) https://truein.com/faqs/general-support/how-to-define-different-categories/ Step 1.2: Assign Categories to Staff (Optional) Assign One by One via Edit: Web Dashboard: Staff Directory > Action Column > Click Edit > Work tab > Time off (Leave) section – Update using ‘Time off/Leave Category’ dropdown Bulk Assign via Bulk Edit Web Dashboard: Staff Directory > Click Bulk/Edit icon > Click Bulk edit- Existing Staff > Select ‘Click Here’ to download the Excel sheet of the existing staff  > Update ‘Leave Category’ Column > Click Save > Click Upload https://truein.com/faqs/employee-setup/how-to-bulk-edit-employee-details/ Step 2: Define Leave Types You can define company-specific leave types such as Privilege Leave/Casual Leave/Sick Leave etc. Please check the following link for setting up the leave types: https://truein.com/faqs/leaves/how-to-setup-leave-types-2/ Step 3: Define Leave Policies You can define the leave policies for each leave type. E.g., Privilege Leave (PL) for permanent staff is 12 per year and will be allotted a month after a staff member completes 180 days of service. The sandwich rule will be applied. An X number of PL can be carried forward to the next year. PL is not entitled to temporary staff and interns. Please check the following link for setting up the leave policies: https://truein.com/faqs/leaves/how-to-setup-leave-policies/ Step 4: Allot Leave Balance to Staff 4.1 For Existing Staff in Truein (before leave policy is setup): Allot/Grant leaves to existing staff one by one or in bulk after leave policies are set up. Please check the following link for the setup: https://truein.com/faqs/leaves/how-to-allot-or-grant-leaves-to-employees-2/ Allot Leave on by one from Manage Leaves 4.2 For New Staff Added (after leave policy is setup): Leave will be auto-assigned based on the leave policy. Admin can manually update it as mentioned in step 4.1. Home Truein Help and Support Leaves How do I set different weekly-off for my staff? How do I set different weekly-off for my staff? You can set the weekly off individually for each staff member from the Web Dashboard. In Truein Web Dashboard: Web Dashboard: Workforce Plan ->Shifts & WO Plan -> Schedule Shift & Weekly Off > Click Download Staff Data > Populate it as per instructions > Click Upload Now, you can view the weekly off for the staff members. Home Truein Help and Support Leaves Is there an option to allot leaves to the staff only after their probation period ends? Is there an option to allot leaves to the staff only after their probation period ends? A probationary period is a defined period from hiring until the newly hired staff member is considered a permanent staff member. If the staff is in their probation period, you can enable the policy “Allow leaves after X days of joining”(X can be customized). You can enable this policy through the Web Dashboard. In Truein Web Dashboard: Method 1: While adding new leave policy Web Dashboard: Leaves > Setup Leaves > Leave Policies > Add Leave Policy > Scroll down and Enable the Policy “Allocate leaves after X days of joining” > Click Save Method 2: While editing existing leave policy Web Dashboard: Leaves > Setup Leaves > Leave Policies > Action Column > Click Three Dots > Edit > Scroll down and Enable the Policy “Allocate leaves after X days of joining” > Click Save Products Open menu Industry Open menu Solutions Open menu Pricing Customer Stories About Us Company Open menu Login Schedule a Demo Why Truein Face Attendance Testimonials Proudly powered by WordPress . Home Truein Help and Support Leaves How to set up multi-level leave approval? How to set up multi-level leave approval? A ‘Multi-Level Leave Approval’ is when a staff member’s leave request has to be approved by a few levels in the company. The levels can vary according to the company’s policies. You can set up multi-level leave approval for your staff either individually (one by one) or in bulk. In Truein Web Dashboard: You need to set the multilevel leave approvers in leave policies. Web Dashboard: Leaves > Setup Leaves > Leave Policies > Add/Edit Leave Policy Now you can set Leave Approval as per your organization requirements. Adding Staff Individually (One by One): Web Dashboard: Staff Directory > Action Column > Edit > Work Tab > Enter Names of the Leave Approvers Adding Staff in Bulk: Web Dashboard: Staff Directory > Bulk upload > Detailed worksheet > Enter Names of the Leave Approvers Products Open menu Industry Open menu Solutions Open menu Pricing Customer Stories About Us Company Open menu Login Schedule a Demo Why Truein Face Attendance Testimonials Proudly powered by WordPress . Home Truein Help and Support Leaves Can we apply sandwich rule for leaves? Can we apply sandwich rule for leaves? When a staff member takes leave for two days or more and a holiday falls in between, the holiday is considered paid leave under the sandwich leave policy. You can apply the sandwich rule by enabling the “Apply sandwich rule” policy from the Web Dashboard. There are two ways to do it. In Truein Web Dashboard: Method 1: While Adding Leave Policy Web Dashboard: Leaves > Setup Leaves > Leave Policies > Add Leave Policy > Enable ‘Apply sandwich rule’ > Click Save Method 2: While Editing existing Leave Policy Web Dashboard: Leaves > Setup Leave> Leave Policies > Action column > Click Three Dots> Edit > Enable ‘Apply sandwich rule’  > Click Save Products Open menu Industry Open menu Solutions Open menu Pricing Customer Stories About Us Company Open menu Login Schedule a Demo Why Truein Face Attendance Testimonials Proudly powered by WordPress . Home Truein Help and Support Leaves How to setup and apply for compensatory off? How to setup and apply for compensatory off? Compensatory off or comp off is a type of leave granted to the staff as compensation for the extra hours worked, usually on a holiday or weekend. Before a staff member can apply for compensatory off, check if the Leave Type and the Leave Policy have been created for the member. The steps to create a Leave Type and Leave Policy are as follows: Creating a Leave Type for a staff member from the Web Dashboard: Web Dashboard: Leaves > Setup Leaves > Leave Types > Add Leave Type > Enter Leave details > Click Add Creating a Leave Policy for a staff member from the Web Dashboard: Web Dashboard: Leaves > Setup Leaves > Leave Policies > Add Leave Policy > Select the leave policy > Click Save Applying for Compensatory Off: Once the Compensatory Leave Type and Policy are created, a staff member can apply for compensatory off. The steps to apply for the same are as follows: In Truein Web Dashboard: Web Dashboard: Leaves > My Leaves > Apply Leave >  Select Leave type (as Compensatory Off) and other details > Click Apply Populate the other necessary fields like First Day of Leave, Last Day of Leave, and finally, click Apply. Home Truein Help and Support Leaves How can I set up holidays and weekly off? How can I set up holidays and weekly off? You can set up holidays and weekly off from the Web Dashboard. In Truein Web Dashboard: You can assign WO on staff category level or site level from Dashboard -> Workforce plan -> Weekly Off -> Add This can also be assigned via bulk  from Scheduler -> Download Bulk Sheet ->  Assign WO in sheet and upload the sheet To assign Holidays you can follow below steps – Admins can set organization level or category level holiday policies. They can define a holiday calendar, setup flexi holidays (which employees will have the flexibility to avail based on the flexi policy setup by admin). WorkforcePlan -> Holidays Policy -> Holiday Calendar -> Add Holidays -> Enter Details -> Click Add or Time Off -> Holiday Policy ->  Holiday Calendar -> Add Holidays -> Enter Details -> Click Add Products Open menu Industry Open menu Solutions Open menu Pricing Customer Stories About Us Company Open menu Login Schedule a Demo Why Truein Face Attendance Testimonials Proudly powered by WordPress . Home Truein Help and Support Leaves Where can I see the leave transactions or the leave history of a staff member? Where can I see the leave transactions or the leave history of a staff member? A staff member’s leave history gives you information about the leaves taken and the leaves available for the staff member. You can see the leave transactions from the Web Dashboard. In Truein Web Dashboard: Web Dashboard: Leaves > Staff Leaves > Manage Staff Leaves > Click Staff Name You can now view the leave history of the staff member you chose. Home Truein Help and Support Leaves How do you change the leave policies for any specific leave type? How do you change the leave policies for any specific leave type? You can change or edit the leave policies from the Web Dashboard. In Truein Web Dashboard: Web Dashboard: Leaves > Setup Leaves > Leave Policies > Action Column > Click Three Dots > Edit > Edit the leave policies > Click Save In the ‘Action’ column, you can select the ‘Leave Type’ you wish to edit. Then, click the ‘Three Dots’ followed by the ‘Edit’ button. Now, edit the leave policies and click the ‘Save’ button. You can approve or reject leaves from the Web dashboard or the User App. In Truein Web Dashboard: Web Dashboard: Leaves > Leave Approvals > Action Column > Click Approve leave or Reject leave In Truein User App: User App: Three Dots > Leave Management > Manage Leaves> Click Approve or Reject Products Open menu Industry Open menu Solutions Open menu Pricing Customer Stories About Us Company Open menu Login Schedule a Demo Why Truein Face Attendance Testimonials Proudly powered by WordPress .
